[30;1m5 | [0m[35mConceptually, Word documents have two `layers`, a *text layer* and a *drawing[0m
[30;1m6 | [0m[35mlayer*. In the text layer, text objects are flowed from left to right and from[0m
[30;1m7 | [0m[35mtop to bottom, starting a new page when the prior one is filled. In the drawing[0m
[30;1m8 | [0m[35mlayer, drawing objects, called `shapes`, are placed at arbitrary positions.[0m
[30;1m9 | [0m[35mThese are sometimes referred to as `floating` shapes.[0m
